-- ========== SECTION A (r_ds_iraction_sharded) : Action & Disposition snapshot (irac_action2) ==========
SELECT
  a.action_id,
  a.oid,
  a.campaign_id,
  a.ircm_terms_id,
  a.sku,
  a.payout_trace,
  a.ircm_category_list_id,
  a.action_date,
  a.batch_id,
  a.adj_reason,
  a.adj_date,
  a.new_status
FROM irac_action2 a
JOIN oids o ON a.oid = o.oid
ORDER BY a.oid, a.action_date DESC;

WITH oids AS (
  SELECT 'pr2527362259' AS oid

-- ========== SECTION B (r_ds_actionlogging_sharded) : Click path / referrer chain (ir_referrer) ==========

  r.*
FROM ir_referrer r
JOIN oids o ON r.oid = o.oid
ORDER BY r.oid, r.ref_date DESC;

-- ========== SECTION C (r_ds_ods) : API payloads & errors (ir_api_log) ==========
SELECT
  l.batch_id,
  l.doe,
  l.reference_date,
  l.endpoint,
  l.status_code,
  l.payload,
  l.error_json
FROM ir_api_log l
JOIN oids o
  ON (l.oid = o.oid OR l.payload LIKE CONCAT('%"Oid":"', o.oid, '"%'))
WHERE l.iram_account_id = 6439962
  AND l.doe >= NOW() - INTERVAL 90 DAY
ORDER BY l.doe DESC;

WITH oids AS (
  SELECT 'pr2527362259' AS oid
